RIG PA'I RGYAL PO THAMS CAD GZENGS BSTOD PAR BYED PA, ,SANGS
RGYAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS SH'AKYA THUB PAS 'DI

GSUNGS MA THAG TU SA CHEN PO RI DANG, RGYA MTSO DANG BCAS PA,
SEMS CAN DANG SNOD NYE BA'I MTHAR THUG PA RNAM PA DRUG TU RAB TU
G-YOS PAR GYUR TO, ,'GRO BA THAMS CAD

RTEN DANG, DMYAL BA'I SEMS CAN THAMS CAD KYI SDUG BSNGAL RAB TU
SBYANGS SHING BDE BA RNAMS KYANG

YID LA BYED CING DE'I TSE DAM PA'I CHOS SPONG BA'I SEMS KYANG MED
PAR 'GYUR NA BDUD SDIG TO CAN

SANGS RGYAS BCOM
